		live_chat.use_this_chat = "games";
	}

<script type="text/javascript">

// JSON that includes affiliate domains
var aff_domains = [\"google\", \"yahoo\", \"bing\", \"facebook\", \"ask\", \"twitter\", \"starsoccer\"];

// Retrive the value of config item PREVENT_AFF_ID_UPDATE
var prev_aff_id_upd = '1';

var ref_url = '';
if (ref_url != "") {
	ref_domain = ref_url.match(/:\/\/(.[^/]+)/)[1];

	if (prev_aff_id_upd != 1) {
		for (var i = 0;i < aff_domains.length; i++) {
			if (ref_domain.search(aff_domains[i]) > -1) {
				$j(document).ready(function () {
					$j.ajax({
						type : 'POST',
						url  : "http://www.paddypower.com/bet?action=update_aff_id",
						data : {
							ref_url : ''
						}
					})
				});
				break;
			}
		}
	}
}

<script type="text/javascript">
        function fireDoubleClickTag() {
            
            var checkCounter = 0;
            
            window.stakeConfirmedInterval = setInterval(function() {
                if (document.getElementById('tick') && typeof(window.stakeConfirmedInterval) !== 'undefined') {
                    clearInterval(window.stakeConfirmedInterval);
                    
                    var stakeAmount = document.getElementById('rb_tot_stake').innerHTML.replace(/[^0-9.]/g, '');
                    
                    var isFirstBet = parseInt(document.getElementById('first_bet_flag').value);
                    var firstBetFlag = Boolean(isFirstBet);
                    var gtmEventName = (firstBetFlag) ? 'first_stake_custom_event' : 'stake_custom_event';
                     
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'cost': stakeAmount,
                        'cust_id': '',
                        'stake_amount': stakeAmount,
                        'event': gtmEventName
                    });
                    
                    delete window.stakeConfirmedInterval;
                }
                 
                checkCounter++;
                 
                 // stop checking if stake has been not confirmed after a minute, 
                 // as it would have timed out by then if it wasn't confirmed yet.
                if (checkCounter > 120) {
                    clearInterval(window.stakeConfirmedInterval);
                }
            }, 500);
        }
        if (document.location.href.indexOf('login_bet_place=1') > -1) {
            fireDoubleClickTag();
        }
    </script>

				document.getElementById("suggestion_link").href = "http://content.paddypower.com/feedback/feedback_form.php?site=lotteries";
			}
		

		
		
		var _gaq = _gaq || [];
		_gaq.push(['_setAccount', 'UA-28094516-2']);
		_gaq.push(['_setDomainName', 'paddypower.com']);
		_gaq.push(['_setAllowLinker', true]);
		_gaq.push(['_trackPageview']);
		_gaq.push(['_trackTrans']);

		(function() {
			var ga = document.createElement('script'); ga.type = 'text/javascript'; ga.async = true;
			ga.src = ('https:' == document.location.protocol ? 'https://ssl' : 'http://www') + '.google-analytics.com/ga.js';
			var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(ga, s);
		})();
		
		
		document.bodyOnLoad.execute();

	</script>

	</body>
</html>
